<div id="review_1293672814" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1293672814" />
    <a title="Jaz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23954973-jaz"><img alt="Jaz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584650592p2/23954973.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1293672814?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jaz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jaz" href="/user/show/23954973-jaz">Jaz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23954973-jaz?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23954973-jaz?shelf=sports">sports</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23954973-jaz?shelf=independent-woman">independent-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23954973-jaz?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1293672814" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10189563300178495729">Another book by Katie McGarry that put a smile on my face! Although I must say this was my least favorite of the <b> Pushing the Limits series </b>, but it still held deep emotions, wisdom and passion.<br/><br/>I buddy read this with my dear friend <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17737927-irena' rel='nofollow noopener'>Irena</a>. She introduced me to this series and for that I am truly thankful.<br/><br/>Haley has left her grandfathers gym after meeting her ex-boyfriend Matt, whom she thought would love her and trust her with anything. Turns out he was a sociopath that didnt believe in the depths</span>
  <span id="freeText10189563300178495729" style="display:none">Another book by Katie McGarry that put a smile on my face! Although I must say this was my least favorite of the <b> Pushing the Limits series </b>, but it still held deep emotions, wisdom and passion.<br /><br />I buddy read this with my dear friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17737927-irena" rel="nofollow noopener">Irena</a>. She introduced me to this series and for that I am truly thankful.<br /><br />Haley has left her grandfathers gym after meeting her ex-boyfriend Matt, whom she thought would love her and trust her with anything. Turns out he was a sociopath that didnt believe in the depths Haley went to become the champion fighter she is. He didnt trust her when she told him his brother had a serious problem with drugs. He beat the sh*t out of her, and she fought back! She hit back! Which broke her and made her swear off fighting, fighters, and the gym!<br />Until she met West Young a rich boy that was kicked out form his home. His family has been dealing with the latest crisis "Rachael's injured legs". It broke him knowing he was to blame, it hurt knowing his family was hurt, but he couldnt stand living under the same roof as his bossy, controlling father that has no heart anymore. HE wanted out... HE needed it!<br /><br />When West and Haley's world collide they start building feelings for each other. West wants to prove to Haley that she's worth fighting for, taking a battle against Matt is the only way he could prove to her and himself that they're worth living, they're worth this life they were given.<br />Haley trains West, she gets her grandpa, cousin Jax, and brother Kaden to help but only under the condition that she returns to the gym, to her old life, to her passion.<br /><br />West has a secret, a secret that will lead to the downhill of his relationship with Haley. Would his father use it against him? Will it be the end of West and Haley?<br /><br />Like I said, this story got me thinking and that's mostly what I enjoyed about it. <br />I liked how it portrayed real life and that no family not rich nor poor is perfect.<br />How every family has struggles and secrets <br />How people could change, when they are shown a little love<br />That breaking the rules is sometimes needed to find yourself, to break your shell and become the person you need to be.<br /><b> Its okay to be lend a hand in life, and its more than okay to grasp it and take the help you are offered </b><br /><br /><br />I cant forget Abby, I loved everything about her in this book. She was just on fire, catching glimpses of her made me happy. She doesnt take sh*t from anyone. Doesnt care who loves her or who hates her. But once she knows someone loves her for who she is and not her outer appearance or how much pot she can give she like Rachael she will do anything for her and I liked that in her.<br />She isnt easy to like, but she sure demands her presence in peoples lives, making them understand and grow accustomed to her presence.<br /><br /><br />I had a little problem with the overall story. I felt the storyline was slow, but yet if you to come think about it all the details were necessary! It was good but it lacked something the other books had which is the Romance. To me their love wasnt special, it was just shallow. I found this book mostly talking about how West found what he really wants and Haley becoming her true self again and following her dreams. They just collided and found it necessary to stick together I guess. Yes, they showed little parts of emotions but it wasnt something deep or heart melting.<br /><br />Both Haley and Wests fathers really pissed me off! Haley's dad was just numb like seriously who would just stand there and allow his daughter to be called a SLUT right in front of your face!! For God's sake do something show some freaking emotion!!!!!<br />And then you have West so called dad who was just cruel to him, and couldnt understand what his son was going through! He was rude, obnoxious, and screwed up! I hated him for kicking West out and only admitting to wanting him back for his mothers sake! CRUEL!<br />But in the end both fathers found the light, and are trying to be the fatherly figure their children require.<br /><br />On the other hand there's Jax and Kaden. It felt weird reading about Jax acting more brotherly than Kaden to Haley! At times when Kaden should stand up for his sister, I found it Jax standing up. That got me thinking that Jax had a crush on her! But luckily he was younger and was just sticking up to her. It really did irritate me to see Kaden hiding behind Jax in situations where he should have been shoving people and moving mountains for his sister and not the other way around<br /><br /><br />The ending was the best part of this story, I found myself on fire just wanting to battle and throw punches left and right esp. at the arena mentioning Rocky and than boom Eye of the Tiger came to mind and I got my boxing gloves and started doing some moves which if anyone saw would probably have thought I was insane! But I just needed to let out some steam LOL<br /><br />Overall, this story was well written and I enjoyed reading it. The Play-list was perfect mix for this novel. <br /><br /><b> "We are stronger together, Haley. Stronger than we are apart."<br /> "I dont feel strong."<br /> "Then I'll be strong enough for the both of us." </b><br /><br /><b> 3 "kickboxing" stars </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10189563300178495729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_858593473" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/858593473" />
    <a title="Caru" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22268349-caru"><img alt="Caru" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486683069p2/22268349.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/858593473?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caru" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caru" href="/user/show/22268349-caru">Caru</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer858593473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3484626948102528472"><b>Rating: ★★★★★<br/><br/>My Opinion Of this Book: LOVED it.<br/>___________________________________________________</b><br/><br/><br/>Damn. I devoured this book in a few hours. LOVED it.<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>THE GOOD.</u>
</b><br/><br/>●<b>West:</b> Oh my gawd, I am in love with West Young. He's got the looks, the humor, the adorable-ness, and the complex, unique personality/perspective. I loved seeing him grow and learn as a character. <br/><br/>●<b>Haley:</b> I liked Haley's character, even though she did get on my nerves sometimes. But in the end, she learned from her mistakes.<br/>I also lov</span>
  <span id="freeText3484626948102528472" style="display:none"><b>Rating: ★★★★★<br /><br />My Opinion Of this Book: LOVED it.<br />___________________________________________________</b><br /><br /><br />Damn. I devoured this book in a few hours. LOVED it.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE GOOD.</u>
</b><br /><br />●<b>West:</b> Oh my gawd, I am in love with West Young. He's got the looks, the humor, the adorable-ness, and the complex, unique personality/perspective. I loved seeing him grow and learn as a character. <br /><br />●<b>Haley:</b> I liked Haley's character, even though she did get on my nerves sometimes. But in the end, she learned from her mistakes.<br />I also loved that she wasn't your typical YA female character. You know, the ones that are all girly. Haley isn't, she's actually more of a tomboy. I mean, she does boxing. Most girls don't. <br /><br /><blockquote>"West?" Haley motions near her eyes. "Attention here, please?" <br />"I wasn't checking out your curves." Though now that it's mentioned... "Go there and I swear to God you'll have to check 'other' when asked if you're male or female."</blockquote><br /><br /><br />●<b>The Side Characters: Ethan, Rachel, etc:</b> I loved how Rachel, Abby, Ethan, and Isaiah made appearances in this book. I so have missed them! They are all incredible.<br /><br />●<b>The Writing:</b> Like I said before in previous reviews on Katie McGarry's works, I worship her writing. She's seriously one of the best of the best YA authors out there. She knows how to make you connect with the characters, feel what they feel, relate with them so much that you feel like you are them. She knows how to bring out emotions out of you with her words. She knows what she's doing. And she does it damn well. <br /><br />●<b>The Plot/Storyline:</b> This book was such an emotional ride filled with raw emotions, showcasing the characters rough pasts, that are realistic.<br /><br /><blockquote>" Don't think of it as falling. Think of it as jumping --- with me." <br />I feel the curve of her smile beneath my lips. "How is jumping better?" <br />"Falling happens. Jumping you choose."</blockquote><br /><br /><b>
  <u>OVERALL</u>
</b><br />I really liked this book, which is why it is my second favorite in this series. <br />I definitely recommend this series -they're great YA romance books!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3484626948102528472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gj2Zo4aua75xgtFTKjFepdb2L4Zgvu0bgABh84orXs+LnBd1jRef+T8OBVjFVwrCDpUQZZ8ON1oOyrrYb9AJFg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('F4T3OS6S5nD/jj5DnJodoovanuzqz2NLE+loUSHzZ/seJXnvJSsSN7EC6khz/EnFU7mhDxV/uQqdI7N6xAgwIg==')})
  }
